1.3.1 Informasjon og relasjoner (5 avvik)
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

First heading is h2, should start with h1

<h2>Kommende kurs</h2>
Start your heading structure with h1
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Page has no main landmark

<body>
Add <main> element or role='main' to wrap primary content

Page has no skip link to bypass navigation

3.3.2 Ledetekster eller instruksjoner (1 avvik)
Testregel 3.3.2 (3.3.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

Form input only has placeholder, no proper label

<input class="filter_search w-input" data-name="Field" fs-list-element="clear" fs-list-field="*" fs-list-highlight="true" id="field" maxlength="256" name="field" placeholder="Søk...." type="text"/>
Add a <label> element with for attribute, or aria-label. Placeholder disappears when typing.
1.3.1 Informasjon og relasjoner (6 avvik)
Testregel 1.3.1 (1.3.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Radio/checkbox group 'radio' not wrapped in fieldset with legend

<input checked="" data-name="Radio 2" fs-list-field="name" fs-list-value="" id="radio-2" name="radio" style="opacity:0;position:absolute;z-index:-1" type="radio" value="Radio"/>
